***соблюдение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдение.html>соблюде́ние</a> (8291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">соблюд-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobljud-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдение.html>соблюде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobljudénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдение.html>соблюде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдение.html>соблюде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдение.html>соблюде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>observance (of laws, customs, etc.), upholding
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:необходимость.html>необходи́мость</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдение.html>соблюде́ния</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́нов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>страны́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пребывание.html>пребыва́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neobxodímostʹ <b>sobljudénija</b> zakónov straný prebyvánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">necessity of observance of laws of the country of stay</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюсти.html>соблюсти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobljustí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблюдать.html>соблюда́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блюсти.html>блюсти́</a></b>)

***собор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:собор.html>собо́р</a> (4758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">съборъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭborŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">συναγωγή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sunagōgḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъborъ</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбор</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic form.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собор.html>собо́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собор.html>собо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собор.html>собо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собор.html>собо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cathedral</li>
<li>council</li>
<li>diet</li></ol>

***соборный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соборный.html>собо́рный</a> (26581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собор.html>собо́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соборный.html>собо́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobórnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cathedral
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соборный.html>собо́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:площадь.html>пло́щадь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sobórnaja</b> plóščadʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cathedral square</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>conciliar, catholic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соборный.html>собо́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> апо́стольская <a href = vnd.unilang:церковь.html>це́рковь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sobórnaja</b> i apóstolʹskaja cérkovʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">catholic and apostolic church</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соборный.html>собо́рное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sobórnoje</b> dvižénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">conciliarism</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">"<b><a href = vnd.unilang:соборный.html>собо́рное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:послание.html>посла́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>свято́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:апостол.html>апо́стола</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иуда.html>иу́ды</a>"</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">"<b>Sobórnoje</b> poslánije Svjatóvo apóstola Iúdy"</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the General Epistle of Jude</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>собра́ние</a> (1612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>собра́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobránije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>собра́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>собра́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>собра́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>meeting, gathering</li>
<li>assembly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:законодательный.html>законода́тельное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:собрание.html>собра́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakonodátelʹnoje <b>sobránije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">legislative assembly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>collection, set</li>
<li>collected works</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a> (1280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собирать.html>собира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gather, to collect</li>
<li>to assemble</li>
<li>to convoke</li>
<li><i>(for a journey)</i> to equip, to prepare</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:собраться.html>собра́ться</a> (996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собраться.html>собра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sobrátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собираться.html>собира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to gather, to assemble <i>mutually reflexive</i></li>
<li>to be about, to make up one's mind, to be going, to intend, to be on the point</li>
<li>to prepare, to be ready to start, to set out</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***сова.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сова.html>сова́</a> (11172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sova</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сова.html>сова́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sová</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сова.html>совы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сова.html>со́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сова.html>со́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>owl
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сова.html>сова́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bélaja <b>sová</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Bubo scandiacus</i>, syn. <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Nyctea_scandiaca" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Nyctea scandiaca"><i>Nyctea scandiaca</i></a></span>) snowy owl</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ушастый.html>уша́стая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сова.html>сова́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ušástaja <b>sová</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>Asio otus</i>) horned owl</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиди́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сова.html>сова́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́ре</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On sidít, kak <b>sová</b> na zabóre</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He doesn’t pay attention to anything (half blind and absent-minded).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>night person, night owl</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In Russian culture, owls are not known for their wisdom; rather, they symbolize daytime blindness and absent-mindedness.
</p>

***совавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:совать.html>сова́вший</a> (6016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совать.html>сова́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sovávšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совать.html>сова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***совать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:совать.html>сова́ть</a> (6016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">совати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sovati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">throw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sovati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">throw, push</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совать.html>сова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сунуть.html>су́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put</li>
<li>to slip, to give</li>
<li>to poke, to stick in</li>
<li>to butt in</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протягивать.html>протя́гивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">protjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пихать.html>пиха́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pixátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заталкивать.html>зата́лкивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zatálkivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соваться.html>со́ваться</a> (9601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совать.html>сова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соваться.html>сова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сунуться.html>су́нуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to try to get <i>(somewhere)</i>, to try to enter <i>(a place)</i>, to poke one's head in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:близкий.html>бли́зко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соваться.html>су́йся</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i blízko sjudá ne <b>sújsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't come near here!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn <i>(to)</i>, to go <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to butt <i>(in)</i>, to poke one's nose <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соваться.html>сова́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совет.html>сове́тами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sovátʹsja</b> s sovétami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to butt in one's advice; add one's two cents' worth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совать.html>сова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***совершённый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершённый</a> (1804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soveršónnyj</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершающийся.html>совершающийся</a> (8227)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершающийся.html>соверша́ющийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soveršájuščijsja</span>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершить.html>соверши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soveršítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to accomplish, to effect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>соверше́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soveršénnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)соверше́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)соверше́нней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">соверше́ннейший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>absolute, complete, perfect</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> perfect, perfective</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершенство.html>соверше́нство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soveršénstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершенство.html>соверше́нства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершенство.html>соверше́нства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершенство.html>соверше́нств</a></b>)
